    WHERE NOT (`c`.`IsDeleted`) AND NOT (`c`.`IsDeleted`)
) AS `t0` ON `g`.`Id` = `t0`.`GroupId`
WHERE NOT (`g`.`IsDeleted`)
ORDER BY `g`.`Id`, `t`.`Id`, `a`.`Id`
